import java.io.File;

// This function delete a file or directory recursively
deleteFile(String strFile) {

 File f = new File(strFile);
 String[] strChildren = null;
 boolean deletionOk = false;
 
 if(!f.exists())
  return true;
              
 if (f.isDirectory()) {
  // Get children
  strChildren = f.list();            
  // Go through each child
  for (int i = 0; i < strChildren.length; i++) {
   deletionOk = deleteFile(new File(f, strChildren[i]).getAbsolutePath());
   if (!deletionOk) {
    return false;
   }
  }
 }
 // The directory is now empty so delete it
 return f.delete();
}

// Main
String baseSuccessMsg = "Delete File Success"; // Do not modify. Assertions might exist on this string.
String baseErrorMsg = "Delete File Error"; // Do not modify. Assertions might exist on this string.
fileS = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\','/');
try {
 File fileF = new File(fileS);
 String file = fileF.getCanonicalPath();
 if(deleteFile(file))
  return baseSuccessMsg + ": " + file;
 else
  return baseErrorMsg;
}
catch(Exception e) {
 return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

EVENT_TRANSACTIONcleanUpTIBCOEnvRegistry-removeNode
Tue Oct 16 22:01:13 PDT 2012 
EVENT_REQUEST
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileInputStream;
import java.io.FileOutputStream;

import org.xml.sax.InputSource; 

import org.w3c.dom.DOMImplementation;
import org.w3c.dom.Document;
import org.w3c.dom.Node;
import org.w3c.dom.NodeList;
import org.w3c.dom.Element;
import org.w3c.dom.bootstrap.DOMImplementationRegistry; 

import org.w3c.dom.ls.DOMImplementationLS;
import org.w3c.dom.ls.LSSerializer;
import org.w3c.dom.ls.LSOutput;
import org.w3c.dom.ls.LSParser;

import javax.xml.XMLConstants;
import javax.xml.namespace.NamespaceContext;
import javax.xml.xpath.XPathFactory;
import javax.xml.xpath.XPath;
import javax.xml.xpath.XPathExpression;
import javax.xml.xpath.XPathConstants;

// Main
String baseErrorMsg = "Removing node error"; // Do not modify. Assertion might exist on these strings.
String baseSuccessMsg = "Removed node successfully";

try {
// Use DOM Level 3
System.setProperty(DOMImplementationRegistry.PROPERTY, "org.apache.xerces.dom.DOMImplementationSourceImpl");
DOMImplementationRegistry registry = DOMImplementationRegistry.newInstance();
DOMImplementation domImpl = registry.getDOMImplementation("LS 3.0");
DOMImplementationLS implLS = (DOMImplementationLS)domImpl;
LSParser parser = implLS.createLSParser(DOMImplementationLS.MODE_SYNCHRONOUS, null);
Document document = parser.parseURI(file);

// Build the namespace context. Will be used by the xPath object.
NamespaceContext MyNamespaceContext = new NamespaceContext() {
 String getNamespaceURI(String prefix) {
  return document.lookupNamespaceURI(prefix);
 } 
 String getPrefix(String namespace) {
  return document.lookupPrefix(namespace);
 }
 Iterator getPrefixes(String namespace) {
  return null;
 }
};

// Get the Nodes and remove them
InputStream inputStream = new FileInputStream(new File(file));
InputSource inputSource = new InputSource(inputStream);
XPath xPath = XPathFactory.newInstance().newXPath();
xPath.setNamespaceContext(MyNamespaceContext);
String expression = xpath;
NodeList nodes = (NodeList)xPath.evaluate(expression, inputSource, XPathConstants.NODESET);
if (nodes.getLength() == 0)
 return baseErrorMsg + ": Node not found. XPath expression is probably wrong.";
for (int i=0; i<nodes.getLength(); i++) {
 Node node = nodes.item(i);
 if (node.getNodeType() == Node.ELEMENT_NODE) {
  Node parentNode = node.getParentNode();
  parentNode.removeChild(node);
 }
 else if (node.getNodeType() == Node.ATTRIBUTE_NODE) {
  Element parentEl = node.getOwnerElement();
  parentEl.removeAttribute(node.getNodeName());
 }
}
Document document2 = nodes.item(0).getOwnerDocument();
inputStream.close();

// Write file
LSSerializer domWriter = implLS.createLSSerializer();
LSOutput output = implLS.createLSOutput();
OutputStream outputStream = new FileOutputStream(new File(file));
output.setByteStream(outputStream);
domWriter.write(document2, output);
outputStream.close();

String successMsg = baseSuccessMsg + ": " + nodes.getLength() + " node(s): ";
for (int j=0; j<nodes.getLength(); j++) {
 Node node = nodes.item(j);
 successMsg = successMsg + node.getNodeName() + " - ";
}
return successMsg;
}
catch (Exception e) {
 return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

import java.io.File;

// This function create a directory
createDirectory(String strFile) {
 File f = new File(strFile);
 
 if(f.exists())
  return true;  
 else
  return f.mkdirs();           
}

// Main
//String baseSuccessMsg = "Directory Creation Success"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.

copyFile(String fileIn, String fileOut) {
 // Do not modify next 2 variables. 
 // Test engineers might have assertion on these strings.
 String baseSuccessMsg = "File Copy Success";
 String baseErrorMsg = "File Copy Error";

 try {
  File fi = new File(fileIn);
  File fo = new File(fileOut);

  // We don't copy directory!
  if (fi.isDirectory())
   return baseErrorMsg + ": Source cannot be a directory !"; 
  
  // If destination is a directory, we'll copy the source file in there

   fo = new File(fo, fi.getName());

  FileInputStream fis  = new FileInputStream(fi);
  FileOutputStream fos = new FileOutputStream(fo);
  
  byte[] buf = new byte[1024];
  int i = 0;
  while((i = fis.read(buf))!= -1) {
   fos.write(buf, 0, i);
  }
  fis.close();
  fos.close();
  return fileOut;
 }
 catch (Exception e) {
  return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
 }

String baseErrorMsg = "Zip extraction validation error";

// Verify that zip file exists
String zipArchivePath = testExec.parseInState(zipArchivePath).replace('\\','/');
String destinationFolder = testExec.parseInState(destinationFolder).replace('\\','/');
f = new File(zipArchivePath);
if (!f.exists())
return baseErrorMsg + ": Zip archive (" + zipArchivePath + ") does not exist.";

// Replace "\" with "/" in the output folder path
/*String destinationFolder = testExec.parseInState(destinationFolder).replace('\\','/'); 
f = new File(destinationFolder);
if (!f.exists())
return baseErrorMsg + ": Destination folder (" + destinationFolder + ") does not exist.";

// Destination folder must be a directory.
if (!f.isDirectory())
{
 return baseErrorMsg + ": Destination folder (" + destinationFolder + ") must be a directory.";
}
*/
// determine the executable extension (G11n team had issue without this).
if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows())
 exe = ".exe";
else 
 exe = "";

// Use TIBCO_JAVA_HOME if exists
f2 = new File(TIBCO_JAVA_HOME);
if (f2.exists()) {
 java = TIBCO_JAVA_HOME.replace('\\','/') + "/bin/java" + exe;
 // this takes care of blank space in path.
// if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows()) {
  //java = java.replaceAll(". [a-zA-Z0-9-_ )(.]*","~1"); // return DOS-like folder name
//  java = "\"" + java.replace('/','\\') + "\"";
// }
}
else {
 java = java_home.replace('\\','/') + "/bin/java" + exe;
}
/*
else {
 java = "java" + exe; // just java, hopefully it will work!
}
*/
//Construct command to issue for unzipping the archive
String command = "";
if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows()) { // handle blank space in path
  command = java + " -Xms64m -Xmx512m -jar util.zip \""+zipArchivePath+"\" \""+destinationFolder+"\"";
}
else {
 command = java + " -Xms64m -Xmx512m -jar util.zip " + zipArchivePath + " " + destinationFolder;
}
return command;

String baseErrorMsg = "Zip extraction validation error";

// Verify that zip file exists
String zipArchivePath = testExec.parseInState(zipArchivePath).replace('\\','/');
String destinationFolder = testExec.parseInState(destinationFolder).replace('\\','/');
f = new File(zipArchivePath);
if (!f.exists())
return baseErrorMsg + ": Zip archive (" + zipArchivePath + ") does not exist.";

// Replace "\" with "/" in the output folder path
/*String destinationFolder = testExec.parseInState(destinationFolder).replace('\\','/'); 
f = new File(destinationFolder);
if (!f.exists())
return baseErrorMsg + ": Destination folder (" + destinationFolder + ") does not exist.";

// Destination folder must be a directory.
if (!f.isDirectory())
{
 return baseErrorMsg + ": Destination folder (" + destinationFolder + ") must be a directory.";
}
*/
// determine the executable extension (G11n team had issue without this).
if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows())
 exe = ".exe";
else 
 exe = "";

// Use TIBCO_JAVA_HOME if exists
f2 = new File(TIBCO_JAVA_HOME);
if (f2.exists()) {
 java = TIBCO_JAVA_HOME.replace('\\','/') + "/bin/java" + exe;
 // this takes care of blank space in path.
// if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows()) {
  //java = java.replaceAll(". [a-zA-Z0-9-_ )(.]*","~1"); // return DOS-like folder name
//  java = "\"" + java.replace('/','\\') + "\"";
// }
}
else {
 java = java_home.replace('\\','/') + "/bin/java" + exe;
}
/*
else {
 java = "java" + exe; // just java, hopefully it will work!
}
*/
//Construct command to issue for unzipping the archive
String command = "";
if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows()) { // handle blank space in path
  command = java + " -Xms64m -Xmx512m -jar util.zip \""+zipArchivePath+"\" \""+destinationFolder+"\"";
}
else {
 command = java + " -Xms64m -Xmx512m -jar util.zip " + zipArchivePath + " " + destinationFolder;
}
return command;

import java.io.*;

copyFile(String fileIn, String fileOut) {
 // Do not modify next 2 variables. 
 // Test engineers might have assertion on these strings.
 String baseSuccessMsg = "File Copy Success";
 String baseErrorMsg = "File Copy Error";

 try {
  File fi = new File(fileIn);
  File fo = new File(fileOut);

  // We don't copy directory!
  if (fi.isDirectory())
   return baseErrorMsg + ": Source cannot be a directory !"; 
  
  // If destination is a directory, we'll copy the source file in there
  if (fo.exists() && fo.isDirectory())
   fo = new File(fo, fi.getName());

  FileInputStream fis  = new FileInputStream(fi);
  FileOutputStream fos = new FileOutputStream(fo);
  
  byte[] buf = new byte[1024];
  int i = 0;
  while((i = fis.read(buf))!= -1) {
   fos.write(buf, 0, i);
  }
  fis.close();
  fos.close();
  return fileOut;
 }
 catch (Exception e) {
  return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
 }
}

// Main
fileIn = testExec.parseInState(fileIn).replace('\\','/');
fileOut = testExec.parseInState(fileOut).replace('\\','/');
return copyFile(fileIn, fileOut);

 }

// Check if file exists

 return baseErrorMsg + ": File ('" + file + "') does not exist";

 return baseErrorMsg + ": File passed is a directory! It must be a file.";

  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot write in file '" + file + "'.";

 return baseErrorMsg + ": User should specify either oldString or propertyFileName or propertyList";

if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
	propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
	if (!propertyFile.canRead()) {
		return baseErrorMsg + ": Property file not found/cannot read it. "+propertyFileName;

	if (!propertyFile.isFile()) {
		return baseErrorMsg + ": property file is not a normal file. "+propertyFileName;

import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileInputStream;
import java.util.Properties;

	Properties getPropList() {
		Properties props = new Properties();
		File propertyFile = null;
		FileInputStream fis = null;
		
		oldStr = testExec.parseInState(oldString.toString());
		newStr = testExec.parseInState(newString.toString());
		
		try {
			if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
				propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
				fis = new FileInputStream(propertyFile);
				props.load(fis);
				
			}
			
			if ((propertyList != null) && (!propertyList.equals(""))) {
				String [] propArray = propertyList.split(",");
				for (int i =0; i < propArray.length; i++) {
					String [] keyPair = propArray[i].split("=");
					if (keyPair.length == 1) continue;
					props.setProperty(keyPair[0],keyPair[1]);
				}
			}
			
            if (!oldStr.equals("")) {
                props.setProperty(oldStr,newStr);
            }
		
		}catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to compute property list."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		finally {
			try {				
				if (fis != null) fis.close();				
			}catch(Exception ioe) {
				//ignore.
			}
		}
		return props;
	}
return getPropList();

import java.io.*;

String baseErrorMsg = "File Read Error"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.
String strFile = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\', '/');

File file = new File(strFile);
if (!file.exists())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + file + "' does not exist.";
if (!file.canRead())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot be read file '" + file + "'.";
if (!file.isFile())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": '" + file + "' is not a file.";

BufferedReader input=null;

try {
    if (encoding.equals("")) 
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(new FileInputStream(file)));
    else 	
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader  
				  (new FileInputStream(file),encoding));

    //BufferedReader input = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(file));
    StringBuffer content = new StringBuffer();
    String line = null;
    /*
    * readLine is a bit quirky :
    * it returns the content of a line MINUS the newline.
    * it returns null only for the END of the stream.
    * it returns an empty String if two newlines appear in a row.
    */
    while ((line = input.readLine()) != null) {
        content.append(line);
        content.append(System.getProperty("line.separator"));
    }
    //flush and close both "input" and its underlying FileReader
    input.close();
    return content.toString();
}
catch(Exception e) {
    return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

import java.util.Properties;
import java.util.Set;

// convert to String because it can comes as Boolean or Integer!
// Replace
// return fileContent.replace(oldStr.subSequence(0,oldStr.length()), newStr.subSequence(0, newStr.length()));
//return fileContent.substring(0, fileContent.indexOf(oldString)) + newString + fileContent.substring((fileContent.indexOf(oldString) + oldString.length()), fileContent.length());

	String replace() {
		String response = fileContent;
        Properties props = propList;
		try {	
            if (prefix == null) prefix = "";
			if (suffix == null) suffix = "";

			if (!props.isEmpty()) {
				
				Set keySet = props.keySet();
				for (Object key: keySet) {
					String name = prefix+(String)key+suffix;
					String  value = testExec.parseInState((String)props.get(key));					
					response = response.replace(name.subSequence(0,name.length()), value.subSequence(0, value.length()));
				}
			}
		}
        catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to replace."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		return response;
	}
return replace();

String baseErrorMsg = "File Write Error"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.

  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + fileHandle + "' does not exist.";

                                 (new FileOutputStream(fileHandle)));
	output.write(content);
	output.close();

	return baseSuccessMsg + ": File '" + fileHandle + "' now contains: \n" + content;
}

baseSuccessMsg = "Replace Validation Success";
baseErrorMsg = "Replace Validation Error"; // there is an assertion on this string
String file = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\','/');
File f = new File(file);

// Check if file exists
if (!f.exists())
 return baseErrorMsg + ": File ('" + file + "') does not exist";

// If fileName is a directory, we fail.
if(f.isDirectory())
 return baseErrorMsg + ": File passed is a directory! It must be a file.";

// If cannot write
if (!f.canWrite())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot write in file '" + file + "'.";

//This can now be optional as users can use propertyFile/List.
// Old string cannot be empty
if((oldString.equals("")) && (propertyFileName.equals("")) && (propertyList.equals("")))
 return baseErrorMsg + ": User should specify either oldString or propertyFileName or propertyList";

File propertyFile = null;
if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
	propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
	if (!propertyFile.canRead()) {
		return baseErrorMsg + ": Property file not found/cannot read it. "+propertyFileName;
	}
	if (!propertyFile.isFile()) {
		return baseErrorMsg + ": property file is not a normal file. "+propertyFileName;
	}		
}

return baseSuccessMsg;

import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileInputStream;
import java.util.Properties;

	Properties getPropList() {
		Properties props = new Properties();
		File propertyFile = null;
		FileInputStream fis = null;
		
		oldStr = testExec.parseInState(oldString.toString());
		newStr = testExec.parseInState(newString.toString());
		
		try {
			if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
				propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
				fis = new FileInputStream(propertyFile);
				props.load(fis);
				
			}
			
			if ((propertyList != null) && (!propertyList.equals(""))) {
				String [] propArray = propertyList.split(",");
				for (int i =0; i < propArray.length; i++) {
					String [] keyPair = propArray[i].split("=");
					if (keyPair.length == 1) continue;
					props.setProperty(keyPair[0],keyPair[1]);
				}
			}
			
            if (!oldStr.equals("")) {
                props.setProperty(oldStr,newStr);
            }
		
		}catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to compute property list."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		finally {
			try {				
				if (fis != null) fis.close();				
			}catch(Exception ioe) {
				//ignore.
			}
		}
		return props;
	}
return getPropList();

import java.io.*;

String baseErrorMsg = "File Read Error"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.
String strFile = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\', '/');

File file = new File(strFile);
if (!file.exists())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + file + "' does not exist.";
if (!file.canRead())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot be read file '" + file + "'.";
if (!file.isFile())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": '" + file + "' is not a file.";

BufferedReader input=null;

try {
    if (encoding.equals("")) 
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(new FileInputStream(file)));
    else 	
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader  
				  (new FileInputStream(file),encoding));

    //BufferedReader input = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(file));
    StringBuffer content = new StringBuffer();
    String line = null;
    /*
    * readLine is a bit quirky :
    * it returns the content of a line MINUS the newline.
    * it returns null only for the END of the stream.
    * it returns an empty String if two newlines appear in a row.
    */
    while ((line = input.readLine()) != null) {
        content.append(line);
        content.append(System.getProperty("line.separator"));
    }
    //flush and close both "input" and its underlying FileReader
    input.close();
    return content.toString();
}
catch(Exception e) {
    return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileInputStream;
import java.util.Properties;

	Properties getPropList() {
		Properties props = new Properties();
		File propertyFile = null;
		FileInputStream fis = null;
		
		oldStr = testExec.parseInState(oldString.toString());
		newStr = testExec.parseInState(newString.toString());
		
		try {
			if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
				propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
				fis = new FileInputStream(propertyFile);
				props.load(fis);
				
			}
			
			if ((propertyList != null) && (!propertyList.equals(""))) {
				String [] propArray = propertyList.split(",");
				for (int i =0; i < propArray.length; i++) {
					String [] keyPair = propArray[i].split("=");
					if (keyPair.length == 1) continue;
					props.setProperty(keyPair[0],keyPair[1]);
				}
			}
			
            if (!oldStr.equals("")) {
                props.setProperty(oldStr,newStr);
            }
		
		}catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to compute property list."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		finally {
			try {				
				if (fis != null) fis.close();				
			}catch(Exception ioe) {
				//ignore.
			}
		}
		return props;
	}
return getPropList();

import java.io.*;

String baseErrorMsg = "File Read Error"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.
String strFile = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\', '/');

File file = new File(strFile);
if (!file.exists())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + file + "' does not exist.";
if (!file.canRead())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot be read file '" + file + "'.";
if (!file.isFile())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": '" + file + "' is not a file.";

BufferedReader input=null;

try {
    if (encoding.equals("")) 
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(new FileInputStream(file)));
    else 	
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader  
				  (new FileInputStream(file),encoding));

    //BufferedReader input = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(file));
    StringBuffer content = new StringBuffer();
    String line = null;
    /*
    * readLine is a bit quirky :
    * it returns the content of a line MINUS the newline.
    * it returns null only for the END of the stream.
    * it returns an empty String if two newlines appear in a row.
    */
    while ((line = input.readLine()) != null) {
        content.append(line);
        content.append(System.getProperty("line.separator"));
    }
    //flush and close both "input" and its underlying FileReader
    input.close();
    return content.toString();
}
catch(Exception e) {
    return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

import java.util.Properties;
import java.util.Set;

// convert to String because it can comes as Boolean or Integer!
// Replace
// return fileContent.replace(oldStr.subSequence(0,oldStr.length()), newStr.subSequence(0, newStr.length()));
//return fileContent.substring(0, fileContent.indexOf(oldString)) + newString + fileContent.substring((fileContent.indexOf(oldString) + oldString.length()), fileContent.length());

	String replace() {
		String response = fileContent;
        Properties props = propList;
		try {	
            if (prefix == null) prefix = "";
			if (suffix == null) suffix = "";

			if (!props.isEmpty()) {
				
				Set keySet = props.keySet();
				for (Object key: keySet) {
					String name = prefix+(String)key+suffix;
					String  value = testExec.parseInState((String)props.get(key));					
					response = response.replace(name.subSequence(0,name.length()), value.subSequence(0, value.length()));
				}
			}
		}
        catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to replace."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		return response;
	}
return replace();

// This routine is written in order to form LGPL zip path which relies on amxVersion and platform
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileInputStream;
import java.io.FileOutputStream;
import java.io.IOException;


//String zipName = testExec.parseInState(amxZip).replace('\\','/');

String zipName="1_linux24gl23_x86.zip";

// look for zip file name
zipName = zipName.substring(zipName.lastIndexOf("/")+1);
String hibernateZipName = "";

//String[] version = {"3.1", "3.2" };
String[] platforms = {
                        "aix53_power",
                        "linux24gl23_x86",
                        "linux26gl24_s390x",
                        "sol9_sparc",
                        "sol10_x86",
                        "win_x86",
                      };

String[] platforms_64 = {
                        "aix53_power_64" , 
                        "hpux112_ia64",
                        "linux24gl23_x86_64",
                        "sol9_sparc_64",
                        "sol10_x86_64",
                        "win_x86_64"                 
                      };

String platform="";
if (zipName.contains("64")) {
    int index=0;
        
    for (String s : platforms_64) {
        if (zipName.contains(platforms_64[index])) {
            platform = platforms_64[index];
        }
    index++;
    }
}else {
    int index=0;
    for (String s : platforms) {
        if (zipName.contains(platforms[index])) {
            platform = platforms[index];
        }
    index++;
    }
}

// copy assemblies 
//String assemplyFolder = testExec.parseInState(TIBCO_AMX_TEST_FUNC_RT) + "/" + platform;

String assemplyFolder = testExec.parseInState(sourceassemblyFolder) + "/" + platform;
File assemplyFolderDir = new File(assemplyFolder);

File[] files = assemplyFolderDir.listFiles();
   
for( File fi : files ) {
    try {
        File fo = new File(destinationassemblyFolder + "/assemblies");
        fo = new File(fo, fi.getName());

        FileInputStream fis  = new FileInputStream(fi);
        FileOutputStream fos = new FileOutputStream(fo);
  
        byte[] buf = new byte[1024];
        int i = 0;
        while((i = fis.read(buf))!= -1) {
            fos.write(buf, 0, i);
        }
        fis.close();
        fos.close();
    }
    catch (Exception e) {
        return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
    }
}

return assemplyFolder ;

import java.io.File;

	Properties getPropList() {
		Properties props = new Properties();
		File propertyFile = null;
		FileInputStream fis = null;
		
		oldStr = testExec.parseInState(oldString.toString());
		newStr = testExec.parseInState(newString.toString());

			if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
				propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
				fis = new FileInputStream(propertyFile);
				props.load(fis);
				
			}
			
			if ((propertyList != null) && (!propertyList.equals(""))) {
				String [] propArray = propertyList.split(",");
				for (int i =0; i < propArray.length; i++) {
					String [] keyPair = propArray[i].split("=");
					if (keyPair.length == 1) continue;
					props.setProperty(keyPair[0],keyPair[1]);
				}
			}
			
            if (!oldStr.equals("")) {
                props.setProperty(oldStr,newStr);
            }
		
		}catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to compute property list."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		finally {
			try {				
				if (fis != null) fis.close();				
			}catch(Exception ioe) {
				//ignore.
			}
		}
		return props;
	}
return getPropList();

import java.io.*;

String baseErrorMsg = "File Read Error"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.
String strFile = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\', '/');

File file = new File(strFile);
if (!file.exists())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + file + "' does not exist.";
if (!file.canRead())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot be read file '" + file + "'.";
if (!file.isFile())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": '" + file + "' is not a file.";

BufferedReader input=null;

try {
    if (encoding.equals("")) 
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(new FileInputStream(file)));
    else 	
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader  
				  (new FileInputStream(file),encoding));

    //BufferedReader input = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(file));
    StringBuffer content = new StringBuffer();
    String line = null;
    /*
    * readLine is a bit quirky :
    * it returns the content of a line MINUS the newline.
    * it returns null only for the END of the stream.
    * it returns an empty String if two newlines appear in a row.
    */
    while ((line = input.readLine()) != null) {
        content.append(line);
        content.append(System.getProperty("line.separator"));
    }
    //flush and close both "input" and its underlying FileReader
    input.close();
    return content.toString();
}
catch(Exception e) {
    return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

createDirectory(String strFile) {

import java.io.*;

copyFile(String fileIn, String fileOut) {
 // Do not modify next 2 variables. 
 // Test engineers might have assertion on these strings.
 String baseSuccessMsg = "File Copy Success";
 String baseErrorMsg = "File Copy Error";

 try {
  File fi = new File(fileIn);
  File fo = new File(fileOut);

  // We don't copy directory!
  if (fi.isDirectory())
   return baseErrorMsg + ": Source cannot be a directory !"; 
  
  // If destination is a directory, we'll copy the source file in there
  if (fo.exists() && fo.isDirectory())
   fo = new File(fo, fi.getName());

  FileInputStream fis  = new FileInputStream(fi);
  FileOutputStream fos = new FileOutputStream(fo);
  
  byte[] buf = new byte[1024];
  int i = 0;
  while((i = fis.read(buf))!= -1) {
   fos.write(buf, 0, i);
  }
  fis.close();
  fos.close();
  return fileOut;
 }
 catch (Exception e) {
  return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
 }
}

// Main
fileIn = testExec.parseInState(fileIn).replace('\\','/');
fileOut = testExec.parseInState(fileOut).replace('\\','/');
return copyFile(fileIn, fileOut);

EVENT_REQUEST
import java.io.File;

String baseErrorMessage="Error finding the installer executable: "; // Do not modify. Assertion on this string exists.

//We are only searching the current folder. No subfolder searches are performed
//There is NO match performed to check if for ex.: if the host OS is Windows and an .exe is present.
//A blind match is done for .exe or .bin. On the first match, the file name is returned.

//Get the list of files in the directory
File f = new File(testExec.parseInState(installerHome).replace('\\','/'));
String[] listOfFiles = f.list();
		
//Run over the list of files in the directory
for (String installerFileName : listOfFiles) {
	//Match 64-bit install .exe or .bin first
	if (installerFileName.endsWith("64.exe") || installerFileName.endsWith("64.bin")) {
	    if (installerFileName.endsWith("64.exe")) {
            return installerFileName;
        } 
        else {
            //If a match is found, return the file name
            return testExec.parseInState(installerHome).replace('\\','/') +
			"/" + installerFileName;
        }
	}
    // Then match 32-bit install .exe or .bin
    else if (installerFileName.endsWith(".exe") || installerFileName.endsWith(".bin")) {
        if (installerFileName.endsWith(".exe")) {
            return installerFileName;
        } 
        else {
            //If a match is found, return the file name
            return testExec.parseInState(installerHome).replace('\\','/') +
			"/" + installerFileName;
        }
    }
}
	
//No match is found
baseErrorMessage+="No Installer executable found";
return baseErrorMessage;

String baseErrorMsg = "Zip extraction validation error";

// Verify that zip file exists
String zipArchivePath = testExec.parseInState(zipArchivePath).replace('\\','/');
String destinationFolder = testExec.parseInState(destinationFolder).replace('\\','/');
f = new File(zipArchivePath);
if (!f.exists())
return baseErrorMsg + ": Zip archive (" + zipArchivePath + ") does not exist.";

// Replace "\" with "/" in the output folder path
/*String destinationFolder = testExec.parseInState(destinationFolder).replace('\\','/'); 
f = new File(destinationFolder);
if (!f.exists())
return baseErrorMsg + ": Destination folder (" + destinationFolder + ") does not exist.";

// Destination folder must be a directory.
if (!f.isDirectory())
{
 return baseErrorMsg + ": Destination folder (" + destinationFolder + ") must be a directory.";
}
*/
// determine the executable extension (G11n team had issue without this).
if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows())
 exe = ".exe";
else 
 exe = "";

// Use TIBCO_JAVA_HOME if exists
f2 = new File(TIBCO_JAVA_HOME);
if (f2.exists()) {
 java = TIBCO_JAVA_HOME.replace('\\','/') + "/bin/java" + exe;
 // this takes care of blank space in path.
// if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows()) {
  //java = java.replaceAll(". [a-zA-Z0-9-_ )(.]*","~1"); // return DOS-like folder name
//  java = "\"" + java.replace('/','\\') + "\"";
// }
}
else {
 java = java_home.replace('\\','/') + "/bin/java" + exe;
}
/*
else {
 java = "java" + exe; // just java, hopefully it will work!
}
*/
//Construct command to issue for unzipping the archive
String command = "";
if (com.itko.util.Utilities.isWindows()) { // handle blank space in path
  command = java + " -Xms64m -Xmx512m -jar util.zip \""+zipArchivePath+"\" \""+destinationFolder+"\"";
}
else {
 command = java + " -Xms64m -Xmx512m -jar util.zip " + zipArchivePath + " " + destinationFolder;
}
return command;

import java.io.File;

// This function create a directory
createDirectory(String strFile) {
 File f = new File(strFile);
 
 if(f.exists())
  return true;  
 else
  return f.mkdirs();           
}

dir = testExec.parseInState(dir).replace('\\', '/');
try {
 if(createDirectory(dir))
  return dir;
 else
  return baseErrorMsg;
}
catch(Exception e) {
 return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

import java.io.*;

copyFile(String fileIn, String fileOut) {
 // Do not modify next 2 variables. 
 // Test engineers might have assertion on these strings.
 String baseSuccessMsg = "File Copy Success";
 String baseErrorMsg = "File Copy Error";

 try {
  File fi = new File(fileIn);
  File fo = new File(fileOut);

  // We don't copy directory!
  if (fi.isDirectory())
   return baseErrorMsg + ": Source cannot be a directory !"; 
  
  // If destination is a directory, we'll copy the source file in there
  if (fo.exists() && fo.isDirectory())
   fo = new File(fo, fi.getName());

  FileInputStream fis  = new FileInputStream(fi);
  FileOutputStream fos = new FileOutputStream(fo);
  
  byte[] buf = new byte[1024];
  int i = 0;
  while((i = fis.read(buf))!= -1) {
   fos.write(buf, 0, i);
  }
  fis.close();
  fos.close();
  return fileOut;
 }
 catch (Exception e) {
  return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
 }
}

// Main
fileIn = testExec.parseInState(fileIn).replace('\\','/');
fileOut = testExec.parseInState(fileOut).replace('\\','/');
return copyFile(fileIn, fileOut);

import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileInputStream;
import java.util.Properties;

	Properties getPropList() {
		Properties props = new Properties();
		File propertyFile = null;
		FileInputStream fis = null;
		
		oldStr = testExec.parseInState(oldString.toString());
		newStr = testExec.parseInState(newString.toString());
		
		try {
			if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
				propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
				fis = new FileInputStream(propertyFile);
				props.load(fis);
				
			}
			
			if ((propertyList != null) && (!propertyList.equals(""))) {
				String [] propArray = propertyList.split(",");
				for (int i =0; i < propArray.length; i++) {
					String [] keyPair = propArray[i].split("=");
					if (keyPair.length == 1) continue;
					props.setProperty(keyPair[0],keyPair[1]);
				}
			}
			
            if (!oldStr.equals("")) {
                props.setProperty(oldStr,newStr);
            }
		
		}catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to compute property list."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		finally {
			try {				
				if (fis != null) fis.close();				
			}catch(Exception ioe) {
				//ignore.
			}
		}
		return props;
	}
return getPropList();

import java.io.*;

String baseErrorMsg = "File Read Error"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.
String strFile = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\', '/');

File file = new File(strFile);
if (!file.exists())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + file + "' does not exist.";
if (!file.canRead())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot be read file '" + file + "'.";
if (!file.isFile())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": '" + file + "' is not a file.";

BufferedReader input=null;

try {
    if (encoding.equals("")) 
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(new FileInputStream(file)));
    else 	
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader  
				  (new FileInputStream(file),encoding));

    //BufferedReader input = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(file));
    StringBuffer content = new StringBuffer();
    String line = null;
    /*
    * readLine is a bit quirky :
    * it returns the content of a line MINUS the newline.
    * it returns null only for the END of the stream.
    * it returns an empty String if two newlines appear in a row.
    */
    while ((line = input.readLine()) != null) {
        content.append(line);
        content.append(System.getProperty("line.separator"));
    }
    //flush and close both "input" and its underlying FileReader
    input.close();
    return content.toString();
}
catch(Exception e) {
    return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

import java.util.Properties;
import java.util.Set;

// convert to String because it can comes as Boolean or Integer!
// Replace
// return fileContent.replace(oldStr.subSequence(0,oldStr.length()), newStr.subSequence(0, newStr.length()));
//return fileContent.substring(0, fileContent.indexOf(oldString)) + newString + fileContent.substring((fileContent.indexOf(oldString) + oldString.length()), fileContent.length());

	String replace() {
		String response = fileContent;
        Properties props = propList;
		try {	
            if (prefix == null) prefix = "";
			if (suffix == null) suffix = "";

			if (!props.isEmpty()) {
				
				Set keySet = props.keySet();
				for (Object key: keySet) {
					String name = prefix+(String)key+suffix;
					String  value = testExec.parseInState((String)props.get(key));					
					response = response.replace(name.subSequence(0,name.length()), value.subSequence(0, value.length()));
				}
			}
		}
        catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to replace."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		return response;
	}
return replace();

import java.io.*;

String baseErrorMsg = "File Read Error"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.
String strFile = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\', '/');

File file = new File(strFile);
if (!file.exists())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + file + "' does not exist.";
if (!file.canRead())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot be read file '" + file + "'.";
if (!file.isFile())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": '" + file + "' is not a file.";

BufferedReader input=null;

try {
    if (encoding.equals("")) 
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(new FileInputStream(file)));
    else 	
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader  
				  (new FileInputStream(file),encoding));

    //BufferedReader input = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(file));
    StringBuffer content = new StringBuffer();
    String line = null;
    /*
    * readLine is a bit quirky :
    * it returns the content of a line MINUS the newline.
    * it returns null only for the END of the stream.
    * it returns an empty String if two newlines appear in a row.
    */
    while ((line = input.readLine()) != null) {
        content.append(line);
        content.append(System.getProperty("line.separator"));
    }
    //flush and close both "input" and its underlying FileReader
    input.close();
    return content.toString();
}
catch(Exception e) {
    return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}

import java.util.Properties;
import java.util.Set;

// convert to String because it can comes as Boolean or Integer!
// Replace
// return fileContent.replace(oldStr.subSequence(0,oldStr.length()), newStr.subSequence(0, newStr.length()));
//return fileContent.substring(0, fileContent.indexOf(oldString)) + newString + fileContent.substring((fileContent.indexOf(oldString) + oldString.length()), fileContent.length());

	String replace() {
		String response = fileContent;
        Properties props = propList;
		try {	
            if (prefix == null) prefix = "";
			if (suffix == null) suffix = "";

			if (!props.isEmpty()) {
				
				Set keySet = props.keySet();
				for (Object key: keySet) {
					String name = prefix+(String)key+suffix;
					String  value = testExec.parseInState((String)props.get(key));					
					response = response.replace(name.subSequence(0,name.length()), value.subSequence(0, value.length()));
				}
			}
		}
        catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to replace."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		return response;
	}
return replace();

if (!fileHandle.exists())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + fileHandle + "' does not exist.";

if (encoding.equals("")) {
        BufferedWriter output = new BufferedWriter(new OutputStreamWriter
                                 (new FileOutputStream(fileHandle)));
	output.write(content);
	output.close();
	return baseSuccessMsg + ": File '" + fileHandle + "' now contains: \n" + content;
} else {

                                 (new FileOutputStream(fileHandle),encoding));
	output.write(content);
	output.close();
	return baseSuccessMsg + ": File '" + fileHandle + "' now contains: \n" + content;
}

baseSuccessMsg = "Replace Validation Success";
baseErrorMsg = "Replace Validation Error"; // there is an assertion on this string
String file = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\','/');
File f = new File(file);

// Check if file exists
if (!f.exists())
 return baseErrorMsg + ": File ('" + file + "') does not exist";

// If fileName is a directory, we fail.
if(f.isDirectory())
 return baseErrorMsg + ": File passed is a directory! It must be a file.";

// If cannot write
if (!f.canWrite())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot write in file '" + file + "'.";

//This can now be optional as users can use propertyFile/List.
// Old string cannot be empty
if((oldString.equals("")) && (propertyFileName.equals("")) && (propertyList.equals("")))
 return baseErrorMsg + ": User should specify either oldString or propertyFileName or propertyList";

File propertyFile = null;
if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
	propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
	if (!propertyFile.canRead()) {
		return baseErrorMsg + ": Property file not found/cannot read it. "+propertyFileName;
	}
	if (!propertyFile.isFile()) {
		return baseErrorMsg + ": property file is not a normal file. "+propertyFileName;
	}		
}

return baseSuccessMsg;

EVENT_REQUEST
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileInputStream;
import java.util.Properties;

	Properties getPropList() {
		Properties props = new Properties();
		File propertyFile = null;
		FileInputStream fis = null;
		
		oldStr = testExec.parseInState(oldString.toString());
		newStr = testExec.parseInState(newString.toString());
		
		try {
			if ((propertyFileName != null) && (!propertyFileName.equals(""))) {
				propertyFile = new File(testExec.parseInState(propertyFileName).replace('\\', '/'));
				fis = new FileInputStream(propertyFile);
				props.load(fis);
				
			}
			
			if ((propertyList != null) && (!propertyList.equals(""))) {
				String [] propArray = propertyList.split(",");
				for (int i =0; i < propArray.length; i++) {
					String [] keyPair = propArray[i].split("=");
					if (keyPair.length == 1) continue;
					props.setProperty(keyPair[0],keyPair[1]);
				}
			}
			
            if (!oldStr.equals("")) {
                props.setProperty(oldStr,newStr);
            }
		
		}catch(Exception e) {
			response = "Fail: Failed to compute property list."+e.getLocalizedMessage();			
		}
		finally {
			try {				
				if (fis != null) fis.close();				
			}catch(Exception ioe) {
				//ignore.
			}
		}
		return props;
	}
return getPropList();

 else

import java.io.*;

copyFile(String fileIn, String fileOut) {
 // Do not modify next 2 variables. 
 // Test engineers might have assertion on these strings.
 String baseSuccessMsg = "File Copy Success";
 String baseErrorMsg = "File Copy Error";

 try {
  File fi = new File(fileIn);
  File fo = new File(fileOut);

  // We don't copy directory!
  if (fi.isDirectory())
   return baseErrorMsg + ": Source cannot be a directory !"; 
  
  // If destination is a directory, we'll copy the source file in there
  if (fo.exists() && fo.isDirectory())
   fo = new File(fo, fi.getName());

  FileInputStream fis  = new FileInputStream(fi);
  FileOutputStream fos = new FileOutputStream(fo);
  
  byte[] buf = new byte[1024];
  int i = 0;
  while((i = fis.read(buf))!= -1) {
   fos.write(buf, 0, i);
  }
  fis.close();
  fos.close();
  return fileOut;
 }
 catch (Exception e) {
  return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
 }
}

// Main
fileIn = testExec.parseInState(fileIn).replace('\\','/');
fileOut = testExec.parseInState(fileOut).replace('\\','/');
return copyFile(fileIn, fileOut);

  return fileOut;
 }
 catch (Exception e) {
  return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();

import java.io.File;

String baseErrorMessage="Error finding the installer executable: "; // Do not modify. Assertion on this string exists.

//We are only searching the current folder. No subfolder searches are performed
//There is NO match performed to check if for ex.: if the host OS is Windows and an .exe is present.
//A blind match is done for .exe or .bin. On the first match, the file name is returned.

//Get the list of files in the directory
File f = new File(testExec.parseInState(installerHome).replace('\\','/'));
String[] listOfFiles = f.list();
		
//Run over the list of files in the directory
for (String installerFileName : listOfFiles) {
	//Match 64-bit install .exe or .bin first
	if (installerFileName.endsWith("64.exe") || installerFileName.endsWith("64.bin")) {
	    if (installerFileName.endsWith("64.exe")) {
            return installerFileName;
        } 
        else {
            //If a match is found, return the file name
            return testExec.parseInState(installerHome).replace('\\','/') +
			"/" + installerFileName;
        }
	}
    // Then match 32-bit install .exe or .bin
    else if (installerFileName.endsWith(".exe") || installerFileName.endsWith(".bin")) {
        if (installerFileName.endsWith(".exe")) {
            return installerFileName;
        } 
        else {
            //If a match is found, return the file name
            return testExec.parseInState(installerHome).replace('\\','/') +
			"/" + installerFileName;
        }
    }
}
	
//No match is found
baseErrorMessage+="No Installer executable found";
return baseErrorMessage;

import java.io.FilenameFilter;
import java.io.File;

// Define the filter to get the post-install errors only
FilenameFilter AntTaskFilter = new FilenameFilter() {
 boolean accept(File dir, String name) {
  return name.toLowerCase().contains(antTaskBaseError);
 }
};

File dir = new File(testExec.parseInState(tibco_test_case_log_dir));
String [] listAntTaskError = dir.list(AntTaskFilter);

String listError = "";
if (listAntTaskError.length == 0)
 listError = "false";
else {
 listError = "Post-Install Task Errors: \n";
 for (int i=0; i<listAntTaskError.length; i++) {
  listError = listError + "\n" + listAntTaskError[i];
 }
}

return listError;

import java.io.*;

String baseErrorMsg = "File Read Error"; // Do not modify. Test engineers might assert on this string.
String strFile = testExec.parseInState(file).replace('\\', '/');

File file = new File(strFile);
if (!file.exists())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": File '" + file + "' does not exist.";
if (!file.canRead())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": Cannot be read file '" + file + "'.";
if (!file.isFile())
  return baseErrorMsg + ": '" + file + "' is not a file.";

BufferedReader input=null;

try {
    if (encoding.equals("")) 
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(new FileInputStream(file)));
    else 	
        input = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader  
				  (new FileInputStream(file),encoding));

    //BufferedReader input = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(file));
    StringBuffer content = new StringBuffer();
    String line = null;
    /*
    * readLine is a bit quirky :
    * it returns the content of a line MINUS the newline.
    * it returns null only for the END of the stream.
    * it returns an empty String if two newlines appear in a row.
    */
    while ((line = input.readLine()) != null) {
        content.append(line);
        content.append(System.getProperty("line.separator"));
    }
    //flush and close both "input" and its underlying FileReader
    input.close();
    return content.toString();
}
catch(Exception e) {
    return baseErrorMsg + ": " + e.getMessage();
}
